API is handled in **pkg/apis/networking/v1beta1/conversion.go**, which contains manual conversion functions for complex backend transformations. The main conversion functions are:\\n\\n1. **Convert_v1beta1_IngressBackend_To_networking_IngressBackend** - Converts the deprecated ServiceName/ServicePort fields to the new Service backend structure\\n2. **Convert_networking_IngressBackend_To_v1beta1_IngressBackend** - Reverse conversion for compatibility\\n3. **Convert_v1beta1_IngressSpec_To_networking_IngressSpec** - Converts Backend field to DefaultBackend\\n4. **Convert_networking_IngressSpec_To_v1beta1_IngressSpec** - Reverse conversion\\n\\nThese conversion functions handle the structural changes where v1beta1 used Backend (with ServiceName and ServicePort fields) while v1 uses DefaultBackend (with Service structure containing Name and Port).\\n\\nAuto-generated conversion functions are in **pkg/apis/networking/v1/zz_generated.conversion.go** and **pkg/apis/networking/v1beta1/zz_generated.conversion.go**.\\n\\nHistorically, Ingress was defined in the extensions API group before moving to networking. Legacy conversion functions for the extensions API are in **pkg/apis/extensions/v1beta1/conversion.go** with similar conversion patterns.\\n\\n## Validation Changes: pathType Requirement\\n\\nThe **pkg/apis/networking/validation/validation.go** file contains the critical validation change where pathType became required in v1. The **ValidateHTTPIngressPath** function enforces that:\\n\\n- **pathType must be specified** (line 428-429): Returns a Required error if pathType is nil\\n- Valid pathType values are: PathTypeExact, PathTypePrefix, and PathTypeImplementationSpecific\\n- Path validation rules differ by pathType\\n\\nThis validation is applied through:\\n- **ValidateIngressCreate** - Validates Ingresses on creation\\n- **ValidateIngressUpdate** - Validates Ingresses on update with compatibility options\\n- **IngressValidationOptions** struct - Provides backward compatibility flags to allow invalid secret names and wildcard host rules from older objects\\n\\nThe v1 validation is stricter than v1beta1, requiring pathType to be explicitly set rather than defaulting to a value.\\n\\n## Default Values\\n\\nIn **pkg/apis/networking/v1beta1/defaults.go**, the **SetDefaults_HTTPIngressPath** function sets the default pathType to PathTypeImplementationSpecific when not specified. This allows v1beta1 Ingresses without explicit pathType to have a default value before conversion to v1.\\n\\nThe v1 defaults in **pkg/apis/networking/v1/defaults.go** do not have a special pathType defaulting function, expecting it to be explicitly set.\\n\\n## Storage Version\\n\\nThe **pkg/registry/networking/rest/storage_settings.go** file configures v1 (networking.k8s.io/v1) as the storage version for Ingress and IngressClass resources in the v1 storage configuration (line 48-51), while v1beta1 is registered as a secondary version.\\n\\nThe version priority is set in **pkg/apis/networking/install/install.go** where v1 is prioritized over v1beta1 and v1alpha1.\\n\\n## Storage and Validation Strategy\\n\\nThe **pkg/registry/networking/ingress/strategy.go** implements the ingressStrategy which:\\n- Defines the validation strategy through ValidateIngressCreate and ValidateIngressUpdate\\n- Handles preparation for create and update operations\\n- Manages reset fields for different API versions (extensions/v1beta1, networking.k8s.io/v1beta1, and networking.k8s.io/v1)\\n- Implements ingressStatusStrategy for status subresource updates\\n\\nThe **pkg/registry/networking/ingress/storage/storage.go** sets up the REST storage with the strategy.\\n\\n## Type Definitions\\n\\nInternal types are defined in **pkg/apis/networking/types.go**, with HTTPIngressPath containing the PathType field as a required pointer to networking.PathType in the internal representation.\\n\\n## Testing and Fuzzing\\n\\nConversion tests in **pkg/apis/networking/v1beta1/conversion_test.go** verify the IngressBackend and IngressSpec conversions work correctly across different port configurations.\\n\\nFuzzing support in **pkg/apis/networking/fuzzer/fuzzer.go** ensures that HTTPIngressPath objects have a valid PathType set when fuzzing the networking API types.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1702,"cache_read_input_tokens":59534,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1702},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"c7759f23-dd6a-4ac9-b4de-28672853aec2","uuid":"56bba3f3-8a2b-42d4-a535-cb86221fb080"}
